*   Power remains heavily concentrated in the hands of President Ilham Aliyev, who has served since 2003, and his family. [freedomhouse](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-0) [freedomhouse](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/1-1) (Freedom House, World Report 2025)

Okay, I will conduct targeted Google Searches to gather the most recent, credible information on "What specific agreements were signed between Azerbaijan and China in April 2025 regarding their comprehensive strategic partnership, and what are the key areas of cooperation outlined in these agreements?" and synthesize it into a verifiable text artifact.
In April 2025, Azerbaijan and China significantly strengthened their bilateral relations by establishing a "comprehensive strategic partnership." [specialeurasia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-0) [eureporter](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [caspiannews](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [commonspace](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3) [jam-news](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [cppcc](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5) [jamestown](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) [caspiannews](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) This development occurred during Azerbaijani President Ilham Aliyev's state visit to China from April 22-24, 2025, at the invitation of Chinese President Xi Jinping [3, 6]. [jamestown](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-6) The key outcomes and agreements are as follows:

**1. Joint Statement on Comprehensive Strategic Partnership:**

*   A "Joint Statement on the Establishment of a Comprehensive Strategic Partnership between the Republic of Azerbaijan and the People's Republic of China" was signed on April 23, 2025 [3, 4, 6]. [president](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9) [fmprc](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-10) [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [jam-news](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-4) [caspiannews](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7) [cppcc](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-5)
*   Both countries view each other as priority, reliable, and mutually beneficial strategic partners, expressing readiness to continuously strengthen mutual political trust, mutual support, and comprehensive cooperation [3, 4].
*   The partnership builds upon a previous strategic partnership established in July 2024 [6, 14]. [wikipedia](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-11) [hagueresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12)

**2. Key Areas of Cooperation:**

*   **Political:**
    *   Mutual support for each other's chosen development paths, safeguarding sovereignty, security, and territorial integrity [3]. [hagueresearch](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-12) [commonspace](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-3)
    *   Azerbaijan reaffirmed its support for the "One China" policy, recognizing Taiwan as an inalienable part of China [3, 4, 6]. [president](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
    *   China supports Azerbaijan's peace agenda [3, 4]. [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [eureporter](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    *   Strengthening political dialogue between the Communist Party of China and the New Azerbaijan Party [3]. [president](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
*   **Economic & Trade:**
    *   Readiness to initiate negotiations on a free trade agreement to deepen cooperation in trade and investment [3, 4, 10]. [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [eureporter](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1) [president](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
    *   Expanding reciprocal access to markets for eco-friendly and high-quality agricultural products [3]. [president](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
    *   Cooperation in renewable energy, contributing to the energy transition and sustainable socioeconomic development [4, 6]. [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [eureporter](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-1)
    *   Jointly establishing safe, stable, and direct China-Europe-China Trans-Caspian express routes [3, 4]. [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8)
    *   Improving customs clearance and cargo transportation efficiency [3, 4]. [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8) [president](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-9)
    *   Expanding investment cooperation in industries such as oil and gas, petrochemicals, green energy, high technology, innovation, and space [5, 13]. [caspiannews](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-2) [caspiannews](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-7)
    *   China supports Azerbaijan's accession to the World Trade Organization (WTO) [4]. [interfax](https://vertexaisearch.cloud.google.com/id/2-8)
